<tr><td width="742"><h3><a href="https://github.com/qgueh2747/djy/blob/master/gb/20/6/30/n12221281.md#1" target="_blank">【新闻热点追踪】党媒承认泄洪 命理师预测7月初三峡有险</a><br></h3><a href="https://github.com/qgueh2747/djy/blob/master/gb/20/6/30/n12221281.md#1" target="_blank"><img width="150" src="https://i.epochtimes.com/assets/uploads/2020/06/b9c7717ca42335395ec8e60a36e4fd90-150x120.jpg" align ="left"></a>大家好，欢迎关注热点追踪，我是尉然。
